 The anti-corruption Bureau has arrested Prahlad Singh, Divisional Accountant, Office of the Executive Engineer, Public Health Engineering Department, in Jaipur, for allegedly taking a bribe of Rs 50,000
 tippaniyan Inspector General of anti-corruption Bureau Vijay Kumar Singh said that Ramratan, contractor of Public Health Engineering Department, had filed a complaint with the bureau
 uske dwaara vibhaag main kiye gaye kaaryon ke liye ek lakh 80 hajaar kaa bhugtan kar diya gaya tha, jisamen se 50 hajaar rupee kii kathith rishwat kii maang diviginal accoutent kar rahaa tha
 After this, the accused again asked for more bribe in order to give the letter of payment of the outstanding rupee bills of Ramratan and pass the bill
 unhone bataaya ki beuro dal kii special branch ne shikaayat ke baad aaropee prahlaad singh ko 50 hajaar rupee kii rishwat lete hue range haathon uske ghar se giraftaar kiya
 Action is being taken under the Prevention of Corruption Act in this case
 bhrashtachar nirodhak beuro ke mahanireekshak vijay kumaar singh ne bataaya ki jan swasthya abhiyantriki vibhaag ke thekedaar ramratan ne beuro main shikaayat darj karai thi
 One lakh 80 thousand was paid for the work done by him in the department, out of which the Divisional Accountant was demanding the alleged bribe of 50 thousand rupees
 iske baad ramratan ke bakaayaa rupee ke bilon ke bhugtan kii patrawali ko dene evam bill paas karwaane kii evaj main dobaaraa aaropee ne or rishwat kii maang kii
 He said that after a complaint by the Special Branch of the Bureau team, the accused Prahlad Singh was arrested from his house red handed taking a bribe of Rs 50,000

 unhone kaha ki maahaul bigaadane waalon ko bakhsha nahin jayega

 iske liye bhaajapa jimmedaar he

 Akshay Kumar's Padman is releasing this Friday
 akshay isamen arunachalam murugannatham kii bhoomika nibhaa rahe hai, jinhone kifayati sanetary pads banaakar lakhon mahilaon kii jindagi badal di
 Now, just like them, two young girls from Mahesana in Gujarat have come out who have made sanitary pads in an organic way
 inhen padagirls kaa naam diya gaya he
 The special thing of the pads prepared by Rajvi and Dhruvi Patel hailing from Mehsana district is that they have been made completely organic
 yani ki ye swasthya or paryaavaran donon ke kaaphi anukool hai
 Rajvi Patel says that the entire pad is made from banana peel, which is completely eco friendly
 aamtaur par sanetary napkin plastic cover ke hote hai, jo ki dikampoj nahi ho sakate
 They are completely decomposed in a year
 skool drop out hai asli pedman, ab chalaate hai sanetary napkin kaa bijnesarajvi or dhruvi donon anand niketan skool main class nauveen kii chaatra hai
 Both girls achieved a lot of results with this thinking
 apane is research work ko anjaam dene ke liye pehle puraa research kiya
 Then, from a company in Vadodara, ordered a thread of banana peel, processed it and made a whole paper
 dhaagon ke is paper ko coton main rakh use sanetary napkin taiyaar kiya gaya
 This project prepared by both of them was so liked that now both girls are known as padgirls only
 dhruvi patel kaa kahana he ki logon ko ye itnaa pasand aayaa ki ab sabhi log hamen padagirls kehane lage hai
 This project of Dhruvi and Rajvi has a lot of potential, it was also tested
 is napkin ko mahesena kii civil aspataal ke gayanek board main diya gaya, jahaan use kaaphi acha rispons mila he
 Now the school is planning to make this eco-friendly pad in the school so that the rural women and girls can use the pads prepared from it
 tvinkal ne bataaya, kaisaa tha unke kising seen par bete aarav kaa riekshaniski keemat bhi zyada nahin he
 Poor women will also be able to buy it comfortably
 isaki keemat 2 se 3 rupye tak he
 The poor women of the village can also make themselves through threads made of banana tree
